   function loadCSS( href, before, media ){
  "use strict";
  // Arguments explained:
  // `href` is the URL for your CSS file.
  // `before` optionally defines the element we'll use as a reference for injecting our &lt;link&gt;
  // By default, `before` uses the first &lt;script&gt; element in the page.
  // However, since the order in which stylesheets are referenced matters, you might need a more specific location in your document.
  // If so, pass a different reference element to the `before` argument and it'll insert before that instead
  // note: `insertBefore` is used instead of `appendChild`, for safety re: http://www.paulirish.com/2011/surefire-dom-element-insertion/
  var ss = window.document.createElement( "link" );
  var ref = before || window.document.getElementsByTagName( "script" )[ 0 ];
  var sheets = window.document.styleSheets;
  ss.rel = "stylesheet";
  ss.href = href;
  // temporarily, set media to something non-matching to ensure it'll fetch without blocking render
  ss.media = "only x";
  // inject link
  ref.parentNode.insertBefore( ss, ref );
  // This function sets the link's media back to `all` so that the stylesheet applies once it loads
  // It is designed to poll until document.styleSheets includes the new sheet.
  function toggleMedia(){
    var defined;
    for( var i = 0; i &lt; sheets.length; i++ ){
      if( sheets[ i ].href &amp;&amp; sheets[ i ].href.indexOf( href ) &gt; -1 ){
        defined = true;
      }
    }
    if( defined ){
      ss.media = media || "all";
    }
    else {

       <h1 class="p-a-title" itemprop="headline">
        The Coolest Jurassic World Cosplay You Have Ever Seen
       </h1>
       <div class="p-a-meta">
        by
        <a class="p-a-author" data-track="navigate:public-profile:article-desc" href="/Joncast" itemprop="author">
         Jonathan Edward Weaver II
        </a>
        
        <span class="p-a-timestamp">
         Posted on
         <meta content="2015-04-14T08:24:34-07:00" itemprop="datePublished"/>
         <meta content="2015-04-17T14:24:27-07:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>

          April 14th, 2015 at 8:24am
         </time>
        </span>
        <small class="p-a-edited">

       <div class="p-a-body pure-u-1 pure-u-lg-16-24" itemprop="articleBody">
        <article class="p-a-text">
         <p>
          With
          <i>
           Jurassic World
          </i>
          set to be released on the 12th of June this year, you'd think that we'd have to wait until at least July for some awesome cosplay related to the latest addition to the
          <i>
           Jurassic Park
          </i>
          franchise. However, I'm happy to tell you that fans have become so excited that there is already a large amount of awesome
          <i>
           Jurassic World
          </i>
          cosplay out there.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Check it out here!
         </p>
         <h3>
          They remember...
         </h3>
         <figure data-id="355512">
          <img alt="They remember..." itemprop="image" src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/images/c_fill,h_640,w_640/t_mp_quality/p7n2c6tqvnffhxwd86wp/the-coolest-jurassic-world-cosplay-you-have-ever-seen-they-remember-355512.jpg" title="They remember..."/>
          <figcaption>
           They remember...
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Seriously, how cool are these raptor suits?
         </p>
         <figure data-id="355523">
          <img itemprop="image" src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/images/c_fill,h_452,w_640/t_mp_quality/kgddltmm2piqr1mlzkgq/the-coolest-jurassic-world-cosplay-you-have-ever-seen-355523.jpg"/>
          <figcaption>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <h2>
          Hitching a ride!
         </h2>
         <figure data-id="355528">
          <img itemprop="image" src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/images/c_fill,h_514,w_640/t_mp_quality/l10ez06ucyb096os9cm4/the-coolest-jurassic-world-cosplay-you-have-ever-seen-355528.jpg"/>
          <figcaption>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Why take a Jeep around
          <i>
           Jurassic World
          </i>
          when you can ride on a raptor?
         </p>
         <h3>
          Epic John Hammond Cosplay!
         </h3>
         <figure data-id="355876">
          <img itemprop="image" src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/images/c_fill,h_512,w_640/t_mp_quality/vhh5uty71pe4uuxm9lg1/the-coolest-jurassic-world-cosplay-you-have-ever-seen-355876.jpg"/>
          <figcaption>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <h2>
          ...Even better John Hammond cosplay!
         </h2>
         <figure data-id="355879">
          <img itemprop="image" src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/images/c_fill,h_430,w_640/t_mp_quality/txtqe8nitgneva8ex9xo/the-coolest-jurassic-world-cosplay-you-have-ever-seen-355879.jpg"/>
          <figcaption>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          These guys even have the ride... impressive to say the least!
         </p>
         <h2>
          The dark side of the park...
         </h2>
         <figure data-id="355880">
          <img itemprop="image" src="http://images-cdn.moviepilot.com/images/c_fill,h_587,w_640/t_mp_quality/mjzafsgpzd4dbm0h4uql/the-coolest-jurassic-world-cosplay-you-have-ever-seen-355880.jpg"/>
          <figcaption>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          These guys chose to capture a less idyllic scene from
          <i>
           Jurassic Park
          </i>
          !
         </p>
         <h2>
          And here is the best
          <i>
           Jurassic Park
          </i>
          cosplay of all time...
         </h2>
         <p>
         </p>
         <div class="b-embed_video">
          <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/KBTV9l64EGA">
          </iframe>
         </div>
         <p>
          Best. Scene. Ever!
         </p>

    if (typeof logData === 'string') {
      return console.log("%c [LiveTracking]: " + logData, 'background: #222; color: #bada55');
    } else {
      console.log("%c [LiveTracking]:", 'background: #222; color: #bada55');
      console.log(logData);
      return console.log("%c [/LiveTracking]", 'background: #222; color: #bada55');
    }
  },
  setTarget: function(params) {
    var id, type;
    if (params == null) {
      params = {};
    }
    if (typeof params === 'string') {
      return this._target = params;
    } else {
      type = params.type, id = params.id;
      if (__indexOf.call(this.supportedTargretTypes, type) &lt; 0) {
        throw new Error("LT: Invalid target type");
      }
      return this._target = [type, id].join(':');
    }
  },
  resetTarget: function() {
    return this._target = null;
  },
  getTarget: function() {
    return this._target;
  },
  trackEvent: function(eventName) {
    var payload;
    payload = this.getPayload();
    if (__indexOf.call(this.supportedEvents, eventName) &lt; 0) {
      throw new Error("LT: Event " + (eventName.toString()) + " is not supported");
    }
    payload.event = eventName;
    if (!this.validPayload(payload)) {
      return;
    }
    return this.sendEvent(payload);
  },
  validPayload: function(payload) {
    var event, target;
    target = payload.target, event = payload.event;
    if (target) {
      return true;
    } else {
      throw new Error("LT: Target is not defined");
    }
  },
  sendEvent: function(payload) {
    var gifImage, paramsString;
    paramsString = this.serialize(payload);
    gifImage = new Image();
    gifImage.src = "https://tower.moviepilot.com/track.gif?" + paramsString;
    this.log('Event data:');
    this.log(payload);
    this.log('Serialized event data:');
    return this.log(decodeURIComponent(paramsString));
  },
  getFullPathWithSegment: function(segment) {
    return "" + (this.browserOrigin()) + (this.browserPathname()) + (this.addPathSegment(segment)) + (this.browserHash());
  },
  addPathSegment: function(segment, options) {
    var key, key_updated, newLTsource, newLTsourceChunk, output, pairStr, params, searchString, val, _i, _len, _ref, _ref1;
    if (options == null) {
      options = {};
    }
    if (__indexOf.call(this.supportedSegments, segment) &lt; 0) {
      throw new Error("LT: segment: " + (segment.toString()) + " is not supported");
    }
    searchString = this.browserSearch();
    newLTsource = this.getPath();
    newLTsource.push(segment);
    newLTsourceChunk = newLTsource.join(',');
    if (searchString === null || searchString === "" || !(typeof history !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; history !== null ? history.replaceState : void 0)) {
      return output = "?lt_source=" + (newLTsource.join(','));
    } else {
      params = [];
      searchString = searchString.substring(1);
      _ref = searchString.split("&amp;");
      for (_i = 0, _len = _ref.length; _i &lt; _len; _i++) {
        pairStr = _ref[_i];
        _ref1 = pairStr.split("="), key = _ref1[0], val = _ref1[1];
        if (key === 'lt_source') {
          pairStr = "lt_source=" + newLTsourceChunk;
          key_updated = true;
        }
        if (key.match(/utm_.+/) &amp;&amp; !options.keepUtm) {
          break;
        }
        params.push(pairStr);
      }
      if (!key_updated) {
        params.push("lt_source=" + newLTsourceChunk);
      }
      output = '?' + params.join("&amp;");
      return output;
    }
  },
  adjustLTParams: function(options) {
    if (options == null) {
      options = {
        keepUtm: false
      };
    }
    return this.browserPathname() + this.addPathSegment('manual', options) + this.browserHash();
  },
  getPayload: function() {
    return {
      referrer: this.browserRefferer(),
      tag: this.getTag(),
      path: this.getPath(),
      user: this.getUserId(),
      url: this.getCurrentUrl(),
      target: this.getTarget()
    };
  },
  getUserId: function() {
    return this._userId;
  },
  getTag: function() {
    var tag;
    if (localStorage.getItem('lt_tag')) {
      return localStorage.getItem('lt_tag');
    }
    tag = this.generateRandomString();
    localStorage.setItem('lt_tag', tag);
    return tag;
  },
  getCurrentUrl: function() {
    return [this.browserOrigin(), this.browserPathname()].join('');
  },
  getPath: function() {
    if (!sessionStorage.getItem('lt_source')) {
      this.processLTSource();
    }
    return sessionStorage.getItem('lt_source').split(',');
  },
  processLTSource: function() {
    var ltSourceString, urlLTSource;
    if (sessionStorage.getItem('lt_source')) {
      return;
    }
    urlLTSource = this.getUrlLTSource();
    ltSourceString = urlLTSource ? urlLTSource.join(',') : 'external';
    return sessionStorage.setItem('lt_source', ltSourceString);
  },
  getUrlLTSource: function() {
    var lt_source_string, params;
    params = this.readUrlParams();
    if (params['lt_source']) {
      lt_source_string = decodeURIComponent(params['lt_source']);
      return lt_source_string.split(',');
    } else {
      return null;
    }
  },
  browserRefferer: function() {
    return document.referrer;
  },
  browserPathname: function() {
    return window.location.pathname;
  },
  browserSearch: function() {
    return window.location.search;
  },
  browserHash: function() {
    return window.location.hash;
  },
  browserOrigin: function() {
    return window.location.origin;
  },
  serialize: function(a) {
    var add, key, s, value;
    s = [];
    add = function(key, value) {
      var i, _i, _len;
      value = value ? value : "";
      if (value.constructor === String) {
        s.push(encodeURIComponent(key) + "=" + encodeURIComponent(value));
      } else if (value.constructor === Array) {
        for (_i = 0, _len = value.length; _i &lt; _len; _i++) {
          i = value[_i];
          s.push(encodeURIComponent("" + key + "[]") + "=" + encodeURIComponent(i));
        }
      }
      return s;
    };
    for (key in a) {
      value = a[key];
      add(key, value);
    }
    return s.join("&amp;");
  },
  generateRandomString: function(length) {
    var tag;
    if (length == null) {
      length = 32;
    }
    tag = "";
    while (tag.length &lt; length) {
      tag += Math.random().toString(36).substr(2);
    }
    return tag.substr(0, length);
  },
  readUrlParams: function() {
    var searchString, transformToHash;
    transformToHash = function(prmstr) {
      var key, pairStr, params, val, _i, _len, _ref, _ref1;
      params = {};
      _ref = prmstr.split("&amp;");
      for (_i = 0, _len = _ref.length; _i &lt; _len; _i++) {
        pairStr = _ref[_i];
        _ref1 = pairStr.split("="), key = _ref1[0], val = _ref1[1];
        params[key] = val;
      }
      return params;
    };
    searchString = this.browserSearch();
    searchString = searchString.substring(1);
    if (searchString !== null &amp;&amp; searchString !== "") {
      return transformToHash(searchString);
    } else {
      return {};
    }
  }
};
  </script>
